(************************************************************************
 Morphisms in the slice bicategory

 We give characterizations for properties of morphisms in the slice
 bictegory. These characterizations only hold when the bicategory is
 locally groupoidal. If the bicategory is not locally groupoidal, there
 still are conditions for proving these properties.
 Note that for esos, we assume that the bicategory is locally groupoidal,
 so that the fully faithful 1-cells are characterized correctly.

 Contents:
 1. Proving properties of morphisms in the slice bicategory
 1.1 Faithful 1-cells
 1.2 Fully faithful 1-cells
 1.3 Conservative 1-cells
 1.4 Discrete 1-cells
 1.5 Pseudomonic 1-cells
 2. Characterizations
 2.1 Faithful 1-cells
 2.2 Fully faithful 1-cells
 3. Constructing esos in slice bicategory

 ************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

Local Open Scope cat.

(**
 1. Proving properties of morphisms in the slice bicategory
 *)
Section ToMorphismInSlice.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b : B}
          {f₁ f₂ : slice_bicat b}
          (α : f₁ --> f₂).

  (**
   1.1 Faithful 1-cells
   *)
  
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
faithful_1cell α

  
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
faithful_1cell α

    
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
p₁, p₂: β₁ ==> β₂
q: p₁ ▹ α = p₂ ▹ α
p₁ = p₂

    
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
p₁, p₂: β₁ ==> β₂
q: p₁ ▹ α = p₂ ▹ α
pr1 p₁ = pr1 p₂

    
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
p₁, p₂: β₁ ==> β₂
q: p₁ ▹ α = p₂ ▹ α
pr1 p₁ ▹ pr1 α = pr1 p₂ ▹ pr1 α

    exact (maponpaths pr1 q).
  Qed.

  (**
   1.2 Fully faithful 1-cells
   *)
  
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
fully_faithful_1cell α

  
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
fully_faithful_1cell α

    
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
faithful_1cell α
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
∏ (z : slice_bicat b)
(g₁ g₂ : slice_bicat b ⟦ z, f₁ ⟧)
(αf : g₁ · α ==> g₂ · α),
∑ α0 : g₁ ==> g₂, α0 ▹ α = αf

    
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
faithful_1cell α
 
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
faithful_1cell (pr1 α)

      exact (pr1 Hα).
    
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
∏ (z : slice_bicat b)
(g₁ g₂ : slice_bicat b ⟦ z, f₁ ⟧)
(αf : g₁ · α ==> g₂ · α),
∑ α0 : g₁ ==> g₂, α0 ▹ α = αf
 
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
∑ α0 : β₁ ==> β₂, α0 ▹ α = pf

      
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
pr1 β₁ ==> pr1 β₂
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
(λ η : pr1 β₁ ==> pr1 β₂,
 DispBicat.disp_2cells η (pr2 β₁) (pr2 β₂)) ?pr1
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
(λ α0 : β₁ ==> β₂, α0 ▹ α = pf) (?pr1,, ?pr2)

      
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
pr1 β₁ ==> pr1 β₂
 exact (fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)).
      
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
(λ η : pr1 β₁ ==> pr1 β₂,
 DispBicat.disp_2cells η (pr2 β₁) (pr2 β₂))
  (fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf))
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           use (vcomp_rcancel (_ ◃ pr12 α)) ;
           [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           rewrite vcomp_whisker ;
           use (vcomp_rcancel (lassociator _ _ _)) ; [ is_iso | ] ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           rewrite <- rwhisker_rwhisker ;
           rewrite (fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map_eq Hα (pr1 pf)) ;
           refine (_ @ pr2 pf) ; cbn ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           apply idpath).
      
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
(λ α0 : β₁ ==> β₂, α0 ▹ α = pf)
  (fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf),,
   to_fully_faithful_slice_subproof Hα g β₁ β₂ pf)
 abstract
          (use eq_2cell_slice ; cbn ;
           apply (fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map_eq Hα (pr1 pf))).
  Defined.

is_invertible_2cell (pr1 p)

    
B: bicat

f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b

Hα: conservative_1cell (pr1 α)

Hp: is_invertible_2cell (p ▹ α)
is_invertible_2cell (pr1 p ▹ pr1 α)

    apply (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hp).
  Defined.

(g₁ g₂ : slice_bicat b ⟦ z, f₁ ⟧)
(αf : g₁ · α ==> g₂ · α),
is_invertible_2cell αf
→ ∑ α0 : g₁ ==> g₂,
  is_invertible_2cell α0 × α0 ▹ α = αf

∑ α0 : β₁ ==> β₂, is_invertible_2cell α0 × α0 ▹ α = pf

        exact (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf).

Hpf: is_invertible_2cell pf
(λ η : pr1 β₁ ==> pr1 β₂,
 DispBicat.disp_2cells η (pr2 β₁) (pr2 β₂))
  (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
     (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf))
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           use (vcomp_rcancel (_ ◃ pr12 α)) ;
           [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           rewrite vcomp_whisker ;
           use (vcomp_rcancel (lassociator _ _ _)) ; [ is_iso | ] ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           rewrite <- rwhisker_rwhisker ;
           rewrite (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map_eq Hα (pr1 pf)) ;
           refine (_ @ pr2 pf) ; cbn ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           apply idpath).

b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b

Hα: pseudomonic_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b

  (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
     (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf),,
   to_pseudomonic_slice_subproof Hα g β₁ β₂ pf Hpf)
 
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: pseudomonic_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
Hpf: is_invertible_2cell pf
is_invertible_2cell
  (pr1
     (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
        (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf),,
      to_pseudomonic_slice_subproof Hα g β₁ β₂ pf Hpf))

b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: pseudomonic_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
Hpf: is_invertible_2cell pf
is_invertible_2cell
  (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
     (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf))

        apply is_invertible_2cell_pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map.
      
B: bicat
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: pseudomonic_1cell (pr1 α)
g: slice_bicat b
β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ g, f₁ ⟧
pf: β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
Hpf: is_invertible_2cell pf
(λ _ : is_invertible_2cell
         (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
            (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat
               Hpf),,
          to_pseudomonic_slice_subproof Hα g β₁ β₂ pf
            Hpf),
 (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
    (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf),,
  to_pseudomonic_slice_subproof Hα g β₁ β₂ pf Hpf) ▹ α =
 pf)
  (is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat
     (is_invertible_2cell_pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα
        (pr1 pf)
        (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat Hpf)
      :
      is_invertible_2cell
        (pr1
           (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map Hα (pr1 pf)
              (from_is_invertible_2cell_in_slice_bicat
                 Hpf),,
            to_pseudomonic_slice_subproof Hα g β₁ β₂
              pf Hpf))))
 abstract
          (use eq_2cell_slice ; cbn ;
           apply (pseudomonic_1cell_inv_map_eq Hα (pr1 pf))).
  Defined.
End ToMorphismInSlice.

(**
 2. Characterizations
 *)
Section FromMorphismInSlice.
  Context {B : bicat}
          (inv_B : locally_groupoid B)
          {b : B}
          {f₁ f₂ : slice_bicat b}
          (α : f₁ --> f₂).

  (**
   2.1. Faithful 1-cells
   *)
  
B: bicat
inv_B: locally_groupoid B
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: faithful_1cell α
faithful_1cell (pr1 α)

• ((α₂ ▹ pr1 α) ▹ pr2 f₂) =
lassociator g₁ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂)
• ((α₁ ▹ pr1 α) ▹ pr2 f₂)

     (((((g₁ ◃ pr12 α)
         • lassociator g₁ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂))
        • (βf ▹ pr2 f₂))
       • rassociator g₂ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂))
      • (g₂ ◃ (pr22 α) ^-1))): invertible_2cell (g₁ · pr2 f₁) (g₂ · pr2 f₁)
β₂:= make_1cell_slice g₂ γ: slice_bicat b ⟦ h, f₁ ⟧
(g₁ ◃ pr2 α)
• (lassociator g₁ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂) • (βf ▹ pr2 f₂)) =
(g₁ ◃ pr12 α)
• (lassociator g₁ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂)
   • ((βf ▹ pr2 f₂)
      • (rassociator g₂ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂)
         • ((g₂ ◃ (pr22 α) ^-1)
            • ((g₂ ◃ pr2 α)
               • lassociator g₂ (pr1 α) (pr2 f₂))))))

    Let p : β₁ · α ==> β₂ · α
      := @make_2cell_slice
           _ _ _ _
           (β₁ · α) (β₂ · α)
           βf
           from_fully_faithful_slice_cell_homot.

    Definition from_fully_faithful_slice_cell
      : g₁ ==> g₂
      := pr1 (@fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map _ _ _ _ Hα h β₁ β₂ p).

    Definition from_fully_faithful_slice_cell_eq
      : from_fully_faithful_slice_cell ▹ pr1 α = βf
      := maponpaths pr1 (@fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map_eq _ _ _ _ Hα h β₁ β₂ p).
  End FromFullyFaithfulSlice.

α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α) → fully_faithful_1cell α
 apply to_fully_faithful_slice.
    
B: bicat
inv_B: locally_groupoid B
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
fully_faithful_1cell α → fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α)
 apply from_fully_faithful_slice.
    
B: bicat
inv_B: locally_groupoid B
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
isaprop (fully_faithful_1cell (pr1 α))
 apply isaprop_fully_faithful_1cell.
    
B: bicat

isaprop (fully_faithful_1cell α)
 apply isaprop_fully_faithful_1cell.
  Qed.
End FromMorphismInSlice.

  Context {B : bicat}

          (inv_B : locally_groupoid B)
          {b : B}
          {f₁ f₂ : slice_bicat b}

                 =

β₁, β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₂, h₁ ⟧
p₁: α · β₁ ==> α · β₂
p₂: β₁ · μ ==> β₂ · μ
r: (p₁ ▹ μ) • rassociator α β₂ μ =
rassociator α β₁ μ • (α ◃ p₂)
r': pr2 β₁
• ((pr1 β₁ ◃ pr2 μ)
   • (lassociator (pr1 β₁) (pr1 μ) (pr2 h₂)
      • (pr1 p₂ ▹ pr2 h₂))) =
pr2 β₂
• ((pr1 β₂ ◃ pr2 μ)
   • lassociator (pr1 β₂) (pr1 μ) (pr2 h₂))
pr12 β₁
• ((pr1 β₁ ◃ pr12 μ)
   • (lassociator (pr1 β₁) (pr1 μ) (pr2 h₂)
      • (pr1 p₂ ▹ pr2 h₂))) =
pr12 β₂
• ((pr1 β₂ ◃ pr12 μ)
   • lassociator (pr1 β₂) (pr1 μ) (pr2 h₂))

      exact r'.
    Qed.

    
B: bicat
HB: is_univalent_2_1 B
inv_B: locally_groupoid B
b: B
f₁, f₂: slice_bicat b
α: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, f₂ ⟧
Hα: is_eso (pr1 α)
h₁, h₂: slice_bicat b
μ: slice_bicat b ⟦ h₁, h₂ ⟧

p₂: β₁ · μ ==> β₂ · μ
r: (p₁ ▹ μ) • rassociator α β₂ μ =
rassociator α β₁ μ • (α ◃ p₂)
β₁ ==> β₂

  Definition to_eso_full_slice
             (Hα : is_eso (pr1 α))
    : is_eso_full α
    := λ h₁ h₂ μ Hμ β₁ β₂ p₁ p₂ r,
       to_eso_slice_lift_2 Hα Hμ p₁ p₂ r
       ,,
       to_eso_slice_lift_2_left Hα Hμ p₁ p₂ r
       ,,
       to_eso_slice_lift_2_right Hα Hμ p₁ p₂ r.

• ((pr1 α ◃ pr2 β₂)
   • lassociator (pr1 α) (pr1 β₂) (pr2 g₂))
pr2 α =
((((pr12 β₁ • (pr1 β₁ ◃ pr12 μ))
   • lassociator (pr1 β₁) (pr1 μ) (pr2 g₂))
  • (pr11 p ▹ pr2 g₂))
 • rassociator (pr1 α) (pr1 β₂) (pr2 g₂))
• (pr1 α ◃ (pr2 β₂) ^-1)

b: B

  (inv_B (pr1 f₁) (pr1 g₂)

g₁, g₂: slice_bicat b
μ: slice_bicat b ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
Hμ: fully_faithful_1cell μ
β₁: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₁, g₁ ⟧
β₂: slice_bicat b ⟦ f₂, g₂ ⟧
p: invertible_2cell (β₁ · μ) (α · β₂)
γ:= make_invertible_2cell
  (inv_B (pr1 f₁) (pr1 g₂) 
     (pr1 β₁ · pr1 μ) (pr1 α · pr1 β₂) 
     (pr11 p)): invertible_2cell (pr1 β₁ · pr1 μ) (pr1 α · pr1 β₂)
H:= pr21 p: (pr2 β₁
 • ((pr1 β₁ ◃ pr2 μ)
    • lassociator (pr1 β₁) (pr1 μ) (pr2 g₂)))
• (pr11 p ▹ pr2 g₂) =
pr2 α
• ((pr1 α ◃ pr2 β₂)
   • lassociator (pr1 α) (pr1 β₂) (pr2 g₂))
pr2 α • (pr1 α ◃ (pr2 β₂ • (pr2 β₂) ^-1)) = pr2 α

     (pr1 β₂) γ · pr1 μ · pr2 g₂)
• (is_eso_lift_1_comm_right (pr1 α) Hα
     (from_fully_faithful_slice inv_B μ Hμ) (pr1 β₁)
     (pr1 β₂) γ ▹ pr2 g₂) = ?t2

        apply id2_left.

  End ToSliceEsoEssentiallySurjective.

  Definition to_eso_essentially_surjective_slice
             (Hα : is_eso (pr1 α))
    : is_eso_essentially_surjective α
    := λ g₁ g₂ μ Hμ β₁ β₂ p,
       to_eso_slice_lift_1 Hα Hμ p
       ,,
       to_eso_slice_lift_1_left Hα Hμ p
       ,,
       to_eso_slice_lift_1_right Hα Hμ p
       ,,
       to_eso_slice_lift_1_eq Hα Hμ p.
